***terminus.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:terminus.html>terminus</a> (55810)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:terminus.html>terminus</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:boundary.html>boundary</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:limit.html>limit</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:term.html>term</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:terminus.html>terminus</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">termini</b> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">terminuses</b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:terug.html>terug</a> (105)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rug.html>rug</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:back.html>back</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <a href = vnd.unilang:compare.html>compare</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">zurück</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb"><a href = vnd.unilang:adverb.html>Adverb</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:teruggrijpen.html>teruggrijpen</a> (98857)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:terug.html>terug</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grijpen.html>grijpen</a></i>.
